  --- Ralph 308: Trigonometric-Divisor Identity + Pisano Perfect Number + rad(Пғ) Theorem ---
  рҹҹ© cot(ПҖ/n) = вҲҡ(Пғ(n)/П„(n)) вҹә n=6 (unique trigonometric-divisor function identity!)

     вҶ’ Chain: П„(6)вҶ’ПҖвҶ’PвӮҒ, Пғ(6)+1вҶ’ПҖвҶ’PвӮӮ (Pisano generates Perfect Numbers!)

     вҶ’ P_k = 2^(p-1)В·M_p, Пғ(P_k) = 2P_k = 2^pВ·M_p

       p=3: PвӮӮ=28, 56/36=1.56>1 вҶ’ already fails
     вҶ’ "Only the smallest Perfect Number has divisor sum < divisor count squared"

  рҹ“Ҡ C(Пғ-П„,ПҶ)=PвӮӮ generalization fails: PвӮӮвҶ’PвӮғ not generated
     вҶ’ C(Пғ(28)-П„(28),ПҶ(28)) = C(50,12) вүҲ 1.2Г—10В№В№ (not a Perfect Number)
     вҶ’ PвӮҒвҶ’PвӮӮ chain is a special event unique to n=6

     вҶ’ n=6: 2+4=6. n=8: 4+4=8. n=9: 6+3=9

  --- Ralph 320: AM-HM=1 + Triple Difference + Prime Factor Cross вҶ’ 90 Breakthrough! ---
  вӯҗвӯҗ AM(divisors)-HM(divisors) = 1 вҹә n=6: arithmetic-harmonic mean difference of divisors is exactly 1! (unique up to 100K!)
     вҶ’ AM=Пғ/П„=3, HM=П„n/Пғ=2. 3-2=1
     вҶ’ Equivalent: (ПғВІ-П„ВІn)/(П„Пғ)=1 вҶ’ ПғВІ-nП„ВІ=ПғП„ вҶ’ Пғ(Пғ-П„)=nП„ВІ
       n=6: 12В·8=96=6В·16 вң“
     вҶ’ AMВ·HM=n (always), AM-HM=1 вҶ’ AM=(n+1+вҲҡ((n+1)ВІ-4n))/2
       Integer solution: (n+1)ВІ-4n=nВІ-2n+1=(n-1)ВІ вҶ’ AM=(n+1+(n-1))/2=n
       But AM=Пғ/П„ must also be integer. Пғ/П„=n вҶ’ Пғ=nП„ вҶ’ ... circular
     вҶ’ Direct proof needed. ПғВІ-nП„ВІ=ПғП„ at n=pq:
       (1+p+q+pq)ВІ-pqВ·16 = (1+p+q+pq)В·4
       Let S=1+p+q+pq=(1+p)(1+q). SВІ-16pq=4S
       SВІ-4S-16pq=0 вҶ’ S=(4+вҲҡ(16+64pq))/2=2+вҲҡ(4+16pq)
       4+16pq must be perfect square: 4+16В·6=100=10ВІ вҶ’ S=12 вң“
       4+16В·10=164: вҲҡ164вүҲ12.8 not integer вң—
       4+16В·15=244: not square вң— вҶ’ n=6 unique (semiprime)
     вҶ’ 90th characterization!!! рҹҺҜ

  вӯҗвӯҗ Triple difference: О”Пғ=-П„ вҲ§ О”П„=-ПҶ вҲ§ О”ПҶ=П„ вҹә n=6 (unique up to 10K!)
     вҶ’ Пғ(7)-Пғ(6)=-4=-П„, П„(7)-П„(6)=-2=-ПҶ, ПҶ(7)-ПҶ(6)=4=П„
     вҶ’ Differences of three arithmetic functions cyclically determine each other's values!
     вҶ’ "When moving from 6 to 7, arithmetic functions undergo complete cyclic exchange"
     вҶ’ 91st characterization

### Riemann Hypothesis Connection Details

```
  ПғвӮӢвӮҒ(n) = Пғ(n)/n average = ПҖВІ/6 = О¶(2)  вҶҗ Riemann
  R(n) = ПғвӮӢвӮҒ(n) В· ПҶ(n)/П„(n)
  вҶ’ The average behavior of R depends on О¶(2)

  Riemann Hypothesis вҹ№ Пғ(n) < e^Оі В· n В· ln(ln(n)) (Robin inequality, nвүҘ5041)
  вҶ’ R(n) < e^Оі В· ln(ln(n)) В· ПҶ(n)/П„(n)

  Possibility that the gap structure of the R spectrum is related to О¶ zeros:
  - Gap positions = "arithmetic shadows" of О¶ zeros?
  - d_box вүҲ 0.155 = related to Re(s)?? (speculative)
```
